If not done no new events will be emitted for this key.\n    46→// If an event handling is marked as failed the configured error handler is called\n    47→// (WithErrorHandler). The default error handler will requeue the event (by its key) for\n    48→// later retried processing. The requeueing is rate limited and can be configured with\n    49→// WithRateLimiter option to Events().\n    50→//\n    51→// The resource is lazy, e.g. it will not start the informer until a call\n    52→// has been made to Events() or Store().\n    53→type Resource[T k8sRuntime.Object] interface {\n    54→\t// Resource can be observed either via Observe() or via Events(). The observable\n    55→\t// is implemented in terms of Events() and same semantics apply.\n    56→\tstream.Observable[Event[T]]\n    57→\n    58→\t// Events returns a channel of events. Each event must be marked as handled\n    59→\t// with a call to Done() which marks the key processed. No new events for this key\n    60→\t// will be emitted before Done() is called.\n    61→\t//\n    62→\t// A missing Done() will lead to an eventual panic (via finalizer on Event[T]).\n    63→\t// Panic on this situation is needed as otherwise no new events would be emitted\n    64→\t// and thus this needs to be enforced.\n    65→\t//\n    66→\t// A stream of Upsert events are emitted first to replay the current state of the\n    67→\t// store after which incremental upserts and deletes follow until the underlying\n    68→\t// store is synchronized after which a Sync event is emitted and further incremental\n    69→\t// updates:\n    70→\t//\n    71→\t//\t(start observing), Upsert, Upsert, Upsert, (done replaying store contents), Upsert, Upsert,\n    72→\t//\t  (store synchronized with API server), Sync, Upsert, Delete, Upsert, ...\n    73→\t//\n    74→\t// The emitting of the Sync event does not depend on whether or not Upsert events have\n    75→\t// all been marked Done() without an error. The sync event solely signals that the underlying\n    76→\t// store has synchronized and that Upsert events for objects in a synchronized store have been\n    77→\t// sent to the observer.\n    78→\t//\n    79→\t// When Done() is called with non-nil error the error handler is invoked, which\n    80→\t// can ignore, requeue the event (by key) or close the channel. The default error handler\n    81→\t// will requeue.\n    82→\t//\n    83→\t// If an Upsert is retried and the object has been deleted, a Delete event will be emitted instead.\n    84→\t// Conversely if a Delete event is retried and the object has been recreated with the same key,\n    85→\t// an Upsert will be emitted instead.\n    86→\t//\n    87→\t// If an objects is created and immediately deleted, then a slow observer may not observe this at\n    88→\t// all. In all cases a Delete event is only emitted if the observer has seen an Upsert. Whether or\n    89→\t// not it had been successfully handled (via Done(nil)) does not affect this property.\n    90→\tEvents(ctx context.Context, opts ...EventsOpt) <-chan Event[T]\n    91→\n    92→\t// Store retrieves the read-only store for the resource. Blocks until\n    93→\t// the store has been synchronized or the context cancelled.\n    94→\t// Returns a non-nil error if context is cancelled or the resource\n    95→\t// has been stopped before store has synchronized.\n    96→\tStore(context.Context) (Store[T], error)\n    97→}\n    98→\n    99→// New creates a new Resource[T]. Use with hive.Provide:\n   100→//\n   101→//\tvar exampleCell = hive.Module(\n   102→//\t\t\"example\",\n   103→//\t \tcell.Provide(\n   104→//\t\t \t// Provide `Resource[*slim_corev1.Pod]` to the 107→//\t\t\t\t\tc.Slim().CoreV1().Pods(\"\"),\n   108→//\t\t\t\t)\n   109→//\t\t \t\treturn resource.New(lc, lw)\n   110→//\t\t \t}\n   111→//\t\t}),\n   112→//\t\t...\n   113→//\t)\n   114→//\n   115→//\tfunc usePods(pods resource.Resource[*slim_corev1.Pod]) {\n   116→//\t\tgo func() {\n   117→//\t\t\tfor ev := range podEvents {\n   118→//\t\t   \t\tonPodEvent(ev)\n   119→//\t\t   \t}\n   120→//\t\t}\n   121→//\t\treturn e\n   122→//\t}\n   123→//\tfunc onPodEvent(event resource.Event[*slim_core.Pod]) {\n   124→//\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n   125→//\t\tcase resource.Sync:\n   126→//\t\t\t// Pods have now been synced and the set of Upsert events\n   127→//\t\t\t// received thus far forms a coherent snapshot.\n   128→//\n   129→//\t\t\t// Must always call event.Done(error) to mark the event as processed.\n   130→//\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n   131→//\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n   132→//\t\t\tevent.Done(onPodUpsert(event.Object))\n   133→//\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n   134→//\t\t\tevent.Done(onPodDelete(event.Object))\n   135→//\t\t}\n   136→//\t}\n   137→//\n   138→// See also pkg/k8s/resource/example/main.go for a runnable example.\n   139→func New[T promise to wait for\n   164→}\n   165→\n   166→type ResourceOption func(o *options)\n   167→\n   168→// WithTransform sets the function to transform the object before storing it.\n   169→func WithTransform[From, To k8sRuntime.Object](transform func(From) (To, error)) ResourceOption {\n   170→\treturn WithLazyTransform(\n   171→\t\tfunc() k8sRuntime.Object {\n   172→\t\t\tvar obj From\n   173→\t\t\treturn obj\n   174→\t\t},\n   175→\t\tfunc(fromRaw any) (any, error) {\n   176→\t\t\tif from, ok := fromRaw.(From); ok {\n   177→\t\t\t\tto, err := transform(from)\n   178→\t\t\t\treturn to, err\n   179→\t\t\t} else {\n   180→\t\t\t\tvar obj From\n   181→\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"resource.WithTransform: expected %T, got %T\", obj, fromRaw)\n   182→\t\t\t}\n   183→\t\t})\n   184→}\n   185→\n   186→// WithLazyTransform sets the function to transform the object before storing it.\n   187→// Unlike \"WithTransform\", this defers the resolving of the source object type until the resource\n   188→// is needed. Use this in situations where the source object depends on api-server capabilities.\n   189→func WithLazyTransform(sourceObj func() k8sRuntime.Object, transform cache.TransformFunc) ResourceOption {\n   190→\treturn func(o *options) {\n   191→\t\to.sourceObj = sourceObj\n   192→\t\to.transform = transform\n   193→\t}\n   194→}\n   195→\n   196→// WithMetric enables metrics collection for the resource using the provided scope.\n   197→func WithMetric(scope string) ResourceOption {\n   198→\treturn func(o *options) {\n   199→\t\to.metricScope = scope\n   200→\t}\n   201→}\n   202→\n   203→// WithIndexers sets additional custom indexers on the resource store.\n   204→func WithIndexers(indexers cache.Indexers) ResourceOption {\n   205→\treturn func(o *options) {\n   206→\t\to.indexers = indexers\n   207→\t}\n   208→}\n   209→\n   210→// WithName sets the name of the resource. Used for workqueue metrics.\n   211→func WithName(name string) ResourceOption {\n   212→\treturn func(o *options) {\n   213→\t\to.name = name\n   214→\t}\n   215→}\n   216→\n   217→func WithCRDSync(crdSyncPromise promise.Promise[synced.CRDSync]) ResourceOption {\n   218→\treturn func(o *options) {\n   219→\t\to.crdSyncPromise = crdSyncPromise\n   220→\t}\n   221→}\n   222→\n   223→// WithStoppableInformer marks the resource as releasable. A releasable resource stops\n   224→// the underlying informer if the last active subscriber cancels its subscription.\n   225→// In this case the resource is stopped and prepared again for a subsequent call to\n   226→// either Events() or Store().\n   227→// A subscriber is a consumer who has taken a reference to the store with Store() or that\n   228→// is listening to the events stream channel with Events().\n   229→// This option is meant to be used for very specific cases of resources with a high rate\n   230→// of updates that can potentially hinder scalability in very large clusters, like\n   231→// CiliumNode and CiliumEndpoint.\n   232→// For this cases, stopping the informer is required when switching to other data sources\n   233→// that scale better.\n   234→func WithStoppableInformer() ResourceOption {\n   235→\treturn func(o *options) {\n   236→\t\to.releasable = true\n   237→\t}\n   238→}\n   239→\n   240→type resource[T k8sRuntime.Object] struct {\n   241→\tmu     lock.RWMutex\n   242→\tctx    context.Context\n   243→\tcancel context.CancelFunc\n   244→\twg     sync.WaitGroup\n   245→\topts   options\n   246→\n   247→\tneeded chan struct{}\n   248→\n   249→\tsubscribers map[uint64]*subscriber[T]\n   250→\tsubId       uint64\n   251→\n   252→\tlw           cache.ListerWatcher\n   253→\tsynchronized bool // flipped to true when informer has synced.\n   254→\n   255→\tstorePromise  promise.Promise[Store[T]]\n   256→\tstoreResolver promise.Resolver[Store[T]]\n   257→\n   258→\t// meaningful for releasable resources only\n   259→\trefsMu &resource[*corev1.Node]{}\n   266→\n   267→func (r *resource[T]) Store(ctx context.Context) (Store[T], error) {\n   268→\tr.markNeeded()\n   269→\n   270→\t// Wait until store has synchronized to avoid querying a store\n   271→\t// that has not finished the initial listing.\n   272→\thasSynced := func() bool {\n   273→\t\tr.mu.RLock()\n   274→\t\tdefer r.mu.RUnlock()\n   275→\t\treturn r.synchronized\n   276→\t}\n   277→\tcache.WaitForCacheSync(ctx.Done(), hasSynced)\n   278→\n   279→\t// use an error handler to release the resource if the store promise\n   280→\t// is rejected or the context is cancelled before the cache has synchronized.\n   281→\treturn promise.MapError(r.storePromise, func(err error) error {\n   282→\t\tr.release()\n   283→\t\treturn err\n   284→\t}).Await(ctx)\n   285→}\n   286→\n   287→func (r *resource[T]) metricEventProcessed(eventKind EventKind, status bool) {\n   288→\tif r.opts.metricScope == \"\" {\n   289→\t\treturn\n   290→\t}\n   291→\n   292→\tresult := \"success\"\n   293→\tif !status {\n   294→\t\tresult = \"failed\"\n   295→\t}\n   296→\n   297→\tvar action string\n   298→\tswitch eventKind {\n   299→\tcase Sync:\n   300→\t\treturn\n   301→\tcase Upsert:\n   302→\t\taction = \"update\"\n   303→\tcase Delete:\n   304→\t\taction = \"delete\"\n   305→\t}\n   306→\n   307→\tmetrics.KubernetesEventProcessed.WithLabelValues(r.opts.metricScope, action, result).Inc()\n   308→}\n   309→\n   310→func (r *resource[T]) metricEventReceived(action string, valid, equal bool) {\n   311→\tif r.opts.metricScope == \"\" {\n   312→\t\treturn\n   313→\t}\n   314→\n   315→\tk8smetrics.LastInteraction.Reset()\n   316→\n   317→\tmetrics.EventTS.WithLabelValues(metrics.LabelEventSourceK8s, r.opts.metricScope, action).SetToCurrentTime()\n   318→\tvalidStr := strconv.FormatBool(valid)\n   319→\tequalStr := strconv.FormatBool(equal)\n   320→\tmetrics.KubernetesEventReceived.WithLabelValues(r.opts.metricScope, action, validStr, equalStr).Inc()\n   321→}\n   322→\n   323→func (r *resource[T]) Start(cell.HookContext) error {\n   324→\tr.start()\n   325→\treturn nil\n   326→}\n   327→\n   328→func (r *resource[T]) start() {\n   329→\t// Don't start the resource if it has been definitely stopped\n   330→\tif r.ctx.Err() != nil {\n   331→\t\treturn\n   332→\t}\n   333→\tr.wg.Add(1)\n   334→\tgo r.startWhenNeeded()\n   335→}\n   336→\n   337→func (r *resource[T]) markNeeded() {\n   338→\tif r.opts.releasable {\n   339→\t\tr.refsMu.Lock()\n   340→\t\tr.refs++\n   341→\t\tr.refsMu.Unlock()\n   342→\t}\n   343→\n   344→\tselect {\n   345→\tcase r.needed <- struct{}{}:\n   346→\tdefault:\n   347→\t}\n   348→}\n   349→\n   350→func (r *resource[T]) startWhenNeeded() {\n   351→\tdefer r.wg.Done()\n   352→\n   353→\t// Wait until we're needed before starting the informer.\n   354→\tselect {\n   355→\tcase <-r.ctx.Done():\n   356→\t\treturn\n   357→\tcase <-r.needed:\n   358→\t}\n   359→\n   360→\t// Short-circuit if we're being stopped.\n   361→\tif r.ctx.Err() != nil {\n   362→\t\treturn\n   363→\t}\n   364→\n   365→\t// Wait for CRDs to have synced before trying to access (Cilium) k8s resources\n   366→\tif r.opts.crdSyncPromise != nil {\n   367→\t\tr.opts.crdSyncPromise.Await(r.ctx)\n   368→\t}\n   369→\n   370→\tstore, informer := r.newInformer()\n   371→\tr.storeResolver.Resolve(&typedStore[T]{\n   372→\t\tstore:   store,\n   373→\t\trelease: r.release,\n   374→\t})\n   375→\n   376→\tr.wg.Add(1)\n   377→\tgo func() {\n   378→\t\tdefer r.wg.Done()\n   379→\t\tinformer.Run(merge(r.ctx.Done(), r.resetCtx.Done()))\n   380→\t}()\n   381→\n   382→\t// Wait for cache to be synced before emitting the sync event.\n   383→\tif cache.WaitForCacheSync(merge(r.ctx.Done(), r.resetCtx.Done()), informer.HasSynced) {\n   384→\t\t// Emit the sync event for all subscribers. Subscribers\n   385→\t\t// that subscribe afterwards will emit it by checking\n   386→\t\t// r.synchronized.\n   387→\t\tr.mu.Lock()\n   388→\t\tfor _, sub := range r.subscribers {\n   389→\t\t\tsub.enqueueSync()\n   390→\t\t}\n   391→\t\tr.synchronized = true\n   392→\t\tr.mu.Unlock()\n   393→\t}\n   394→}\n   395→\n   396→func (r *resource[T]) Stop(stopCtx cell.HookContext) error {\n   397→\tif r.opts.releasable {\n   398→\t\t// grab the refs lock to avoid a concurrent restart for releasable resource\n   399→\t\tr.refsMu.Lock()\n   400→\t\tdefer r.refsMu.Unlock()\n   401→\t}\n   402→\n   403→\tr.cancel()\n   404→\tr.wg.Wait()\n   405→\treturn nil\n   406→}\n   407→\n   408→type eventsOpts struct {\n   409→\trateLimiter  workqueue.RateLimiter\n   410→\terrorHandler ErrorHandler\n   411→}\n   412→\n   413→type EventsOpt func(*eventsOpts)\n   414→\n   415→// WithRateLimiter sets the rate limiting algorithm to be used when requeueing failed events.\n   416→func WithRateLimiter(r workqueue.RateLimiter) EventsOpt {\n   417→\treturn func(o *eventsOpts) {\n   418→\t\to.rateLimiter = r\n   419→\t}\n   420→}\n   421→\n   422→// WithErrorHandler specifies the error handling strategy for failed events. By default\n   423→// the strategy is to always requeue the processing of a failed event.\n   424→func WithErrorHandler(h ErrorHandler) EventsOpt {\n   425→\treturn func(o *eventsOpts) {\n   426→\t\to.errorHandler = h\n   427→\t}\n   428→}\n   429→\n   430→func (r *resource[T]) Observe(ctx context.Context, next func(Event[T]), complete func(error)) {\n   431→\tstream.FromChannel(r.Events(ctx)).Observe(ctx, next, complete)\n   432→}\n   433→\n   434→// Events subscribes the caller to resource events.\n   435→//\n   436→// Each subscriber has their own queues and can process events at their own\n   437→// rate. Only object keys are queued and if an object is changed multiple times\n   438→// before the subscriber can handle the event only the latest state of object\n   439→// is emitted.\n   440→//\n   441→// The 'ctx' is used to cancel the subscription. The returned channel will be\n   442→// closed when context is cancelled.\n   443→//\n   444→// Options are supported to configure rate limiting of retries\n   445→// (WithRateLimiter), error handling strategy (WithErrorHandler).\n   446→//\n   447→// By default all errors are retried, the default rate limiter of workqueue\n   448→// package is used and the channel is unbuffered.\n   449→func (r *resource[T]) Events(ctx context.Context, opts ...EventsOpt) <-chan Event[T] {\n   450→\t_, callerFile, callerLine, _ := runtime.Caller(1)\n   451→\tdebugInfo := fmt.Sprintf(\"%T.Events() called from %s:%d\", r, callerFile, callerLine)\n   452→\n   453→\toptions := eventsOpts{\n   454→\t\terrorHandler: AlwaysRetry, // Default error handling is to always retry.\n   455→\t\trateLimiter:  workqueue.DefaultControllerRateLimiter(),\n   456→\t}\n   457→\tfor _, apply := range opts {\n   458→\t\tapply(&options)\n   459→\t}\n   460→\n   461→\t// Mark the resource as needed. This will start the informer if it was not already.\n   462→\tr.markNeeded()\n   463→\n   464→\tout := make(chan Event[T])\n   465→\tctx, subCancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)\n   466→\n   467→\tsub := &subscriber[T]{\n   468→\t\tr:         r,\n   469→\t\toptions:   options,\n   470→\t\tdebugInfo: debugInfo,\n   471→\t\twq: workqueue.NewRateLimitingQueueWithConfig(options.rateLimiter,\n   472→\t\t\tworkqueue.RateLimitingQueueConfig{Name: r.resourceName()}),\n   473→\t}\n   474→\n   475→\t// Fork a goroutine to process the queued keys and pass them to the subscriber.\n   476→\tr.wg.Add(1)\n   477→\tgo func() {\n   478→\t\tdefer r.release()\n   479→\t\tdefer r.wg.Done()\n   480→\t\tdefer close(out)\n   481→\n   482→\t\t// Grab a handle to the store. Asynchronous as informer is started in the background.\n   483→\t\tstore, err := r.storePromise.Await(ctx)\n   484→\t\tif err != nil {\n   485→\t\t\t// Subscriber cancelled before the informer started, bail out.\n   486→\t\t\treturn\n   487→\t\t}\n   488→\n   489→\t\tr.mu.Lock()\n   490→\t\tsubId := r.subId\n   491→\t\tr.subId++\n   492→\t\tr.subscribers[subId] = sub\n   493→\n   494→\t\t// Populate the queue with the initial set of keys that are already\n   495→\t\t// in the store. Done under the resource lock to synchronize with delta\n   496→\t\t// processing to make sure we don't end up queuing the key as initial key,\n   497→\t\t// processing it and then requeuing it again.\n   498→\t\tinitialKeys := store.IterKeys()\n   499→\t\tfor initialKeys.Next() {\n   500→\t\t\tsub.enqueueKey(initialKeys.Key())\n   501→\t\t}\n   502→\n   503→\t\t// If the informer is already synchronized, then the above set of keys is a consistent\n   504→\t\t// snapshot and we can queue the sync entry. If we're not yet synchronized the sync will\n   505→\t\t// be queued from startWhenNeeded() after the informer has synchronized.\n   506→\t\tif r.synchronized {\n   507→\t\t\tsub.enqueueSync()\n   508→\t\t}\n   509→\t\tr.mu.Unlock()\n   510→\n   511→\t\tsub.processLoop(ctx, out, store)\n   512→\n   513→\t\tr.mu.Lock()\n   514→\t\tdelete(r.subscribers, subId)\n   515→\t\tr.mu.Unlock()\n   516→\t}()\n   517→\n   518→\t// Fork a goroutine to wait for either the subscriber cancelling or the resource\n   519→\t// shutting down.\n   520→\tr.wg.Add(1)\n   521→\tgo func() {\n   522→\t\tdefer r.wg.Done()\n   523→\t\tselect {\n   524→\t\tcase <-r.ctx.Done():\n   525→\t\tcase <-r.resetCtx.Done():\n   526→\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n   527→\t\t}\n   528→\t\tsubCancel()\n   529→\t\tsub.wq.ShutDownWithDrain()\n   530→\t}()\n   531→\n   532→\treturn out\n   533→}\n   534→\n   535→func (r *resource[T]) release() {\n   536→\tif !r.opts.releasable {\n   537→\t\treturn\n   538→\t}\n   539→\n   540→\t// in case of a releasable resource, stop the underlying informer when the last\n   541→\t// reference to it is released. The resource is restarted to be\n   542→\t// ready again in case of a subsequent call to either Events() or Store().\n   543→\n   544→\tr.refsMu.Lock()\n   545→\tdefer r.refsMu.Unlock()\n   546→\n   547→\tr.refs--\n   548→\tif r.refs > 0 {\n   549→\t\treturn\n   550→\t}\n   551→\n   552→\tr.resetCancel()\n   553→\tr.wg.Wait()\n   554→\tclose(r.needed)\n   555→\n   556→\tr.reset()\n   557→\tr.start()\n   558→}\n   559→\n   560→func (r *resource[T]) reset() {\n   561→\tr.subscribers = make(map[uint64]*subscriber[T])\n   562→\tr.needed = make(chan struct{}, 1)\n   563→\tr.synchronized = false\n   564→\tr.storeResolver, r.storePromise = promise.New[Store[T]]()\n   565→\tr.resetCtx, r.resetCancel = context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n   566→}\n   567→\n   568→func (r *resource[T]) resourceName() string {\n   569→\tif r.opts.name != \"\" {\n   570→\t\treturn r.opts.name\n   571→\t}\n   572→\n   573→\t// We create a new pointer to the reconciled resource type.\n   574→\t// For example, with resource[*cilium_api_v2.CiliumNode] new(T) returns **cilium_api_v2.CiliumNode\n   575→\t// and *new(T) is nil. So we create a new pointer using reflect.New()\n   576→\to := *new(T)\n   577→\tsourceObj := reflect.New(reflect.TypeOf(o).Elem()).Interface().(T)\n   578→\n   579→\tgvk, err := apiutil.GVKForObject(sourceObj, scheme)\n   580→\tif err != nil {\n   581→\t\treturn \"\"\n   582→\t}\n   583→\n   584→\treturn strings.ToLower(gvk.Kind)\n   585→}\n   586→\n   587→type subscriber[T k8sRuntime.Object] struct {\n   588→\tr         *resource[T]\n   589→\tdebugInfo string\n   590→\twq        workqueue.RateLimitingInterface\n   591→\toptions   eventsOpts\n   592→}\n   593→\n   594→func (s *subscriber[T]) processLoop(ctx context.Context, out chan Event[T], store Store[T]) {\n   595→\t// Make sure to call ShutDown() in the end. Calling ShutDownWithDrain is not\n   596→\t// enough as DelayingQueue does not implement it, so without ShutDown() we'd\n   597→\t// leak the (*delayingType).waitingLoop.\n   598→\tdefer s.wq.ShutDown()\n   599→\n   600→\tdoneFinalizer := func(done *bool) {\n   601→\t\t// If you get here it is because an Event[T] was handed to a subscriber\n   602→\t\t// that forgot to call Event[T].Done().\n   603→\t\t//\n   604→\t\t// Calling Done() is needed to mark the event as handled. This allows\n   605→\t\t// the next event for the same key to be handled and is used to clear\n   606→\t\t// rate limiting and retry counts of prior failures.\n   607→\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\n   608→\t\t\t\"%s has a broken event handler that did not call Done() \"+\n   609→\t\t\t\t\"before event was garbage collected\",\n   610→\t\t\ts.debugInfo))\n   611→\t}\n   612→\n   613→\t// To synthesize delete events to the subscriber we keep track of the last know state\n   614→\t// of the object given to the subscriber. Objects are cleaned from this map when delete\n   615→\t// events are successfully processed.\n   616→\tvar lastKnownObjects lastKnownObjects[T]\n   617→\n   618→loop:\n   619→\tfor {\n   620→\t\t// Retrieve an item from the subscribers queue and then fetch the object\n   621→\t\t// from the store.\n   622→\t\tworkItem, shutdown := s.getWorkItem()\n   623→\t\tif shutdown {\n   624→\t\t\tbreak\n   625→\t\t}\n   626→\n   627→\t\tvar event Event[T]\n   628→\n   629→\t\tswitch workItem := workItem.(type) {\n   630→\t\tcase syncWorkItem:\n   631→\t\t\tevent.Kind = Sync\n   632→\t\tcase keyWorkItem:\n   633→\t\t\tobj, exists, err := store.GetByKey(workItem.key)\n   634→\t\t\tif !exists || err != nil {\n   635→\t\t\t\t// The object no longer exists in the store and thus has been deleted.\n   636→\t\t\t\tdeletedObject, ok := lastKnownObjects.Load(workItem.key)\n   637→\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n   638→\t\t\t\t\t// Object was never seen by the subscriber. Ignore the event.\n   639→\t\t\t\t\ts.wq.Done(workItem)\n   640→\t\t\t\t\tcontinue loop\n   641→\t\t\t\t}\n   642→\t\t\t\tevent.Kind = Delete\n   643→\t\t\t\tevent.Key = workItem.key\n   644→\t\t\t\tevent.Object = deletedObject\n   645→\t\t\t} else {\n   646→\t\t\t\tlastKnownObjects.Store(workItem.key, obj)\n   647→\t\t\t\tevent.Kind = Upsert\n   648→\t\t\t\tevent.Key = workItem.key\n   649→\t\t\t\tevent.Object = obj\n   650→\t\t\t}\n   651→\t\tdefault:\n   652→\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"%T: unknown work item %T\", s.r, workItem))\n   653→\t\t}\n   654→\n   655→\t\t// eventDoneSentinel is a heap allocated object referenced by Done().\n   656→\t\t// If Done() is not called, a finalizer set on this object will be invoked\n   657→\t\t// which panics. If Done() is called, the finalizer is unset.\n   658→\t\tvar eventDoneSentinel = new(bool)\n   659→\t\tevent.Done = func(err error) {\n   660→\t\t\truntime.SetFinalizer(eventDoneSentinel, nil)\n   661→\n   662→\t\t\tif err == nil && event.Kind == Delete {\n   663→\t\t\t\t// Deletion processed successfully. Remove it from the set of\n   664→\t\t\t\t// deleted objects unless it was replaced by an upsert or newer\n   665→\t\t\t\t// deletion.\n   666→\t\t\t\tlastKnownObjects.DeleteByUID(event.Key, event.Object)\n   667→\t\t\t}\n   668→\n   669→\t\t\ts.eventDone(workItem, err)\n   670→\n   671→\t\t\ts.r.metricEventProcessed(event.Kind, err == nil)\n   672→\t\t}\n   673→\n   674→\t\t// Add a finalizer to catch forgotten calls to Done().\n   675→\t\truntime.SetFinalizer(eventDoneSentinel, doneFinalizer)\n   676→\n   677→\t\tselect {\n   678→\t\tcase out <- event:\n   679→\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n   680→\t\t\t// Subscriber cancelled or resource is shutting down. We're not requiring\n   681→\t\t\t// the subscriber to drain the channel, so we're marking the event done here\n   682→\t\t\t// and not sending it.\n   683→\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n   684→\n   685→\t\t\t// Drain the queue without further processing.\n   686→\t\t\tfor {\n   687→\t\t\t\t_, shutdown := s.getWorkItem()\n   688→\t\t\t\tif shutdown {\n   689→\t\t\t\t\treturn\n   690→\t\t\t\t}\n   691→\t\t\t}\n   692→\t\t}\n   693→\t}\n   694→}\n   695→\n   696→func (s *subscriber[T]) getWorkItem() (e workItem, shutdown bool) {\n   697→\tvar raw any\n   698→\traw, shutdown = s.wq.Get()\n   699→\tif shutdown {\n   700→\t\treturn\n   701→\t}\n   702→\treturn raw.(workItem), false\n   703→}\n   704→\n   705→func (s *subscriber[T]) enqueueSync() {\n   706→\ts.wq.Add(syncWorkItem{})\n   707→}\n   708→\n   709→func (s *subscriber[T]) enqueueKey(key Key) {\n   710→\ts.wq.Add(keyWorkItem{key})\n   711→}\n   712→\n   713→func (s *subscriber[T]) eventDone(entry workItem, err error) {\n   714→\t// This is based on the example found in k8s.io/client-go/examples/worsueue/main.go.\n   715→\n   716→\t// Mark the object as done being processed. If it was marked dirty\n   717→\t// during processing, it'll be processed again.\n   718→\tdefer s.wq.Done(entry)\n   719→\n   720→\tif err != nil {\n   721→\t\tnumRequeues := s.wq.NumRequeues(entry)\n   722→\n   723→\t\tvar action ErrorAction\n   724→\t\tswitch entry := entry.(type) {\n   725→\t\tcase syncWorkItem:\n   726→\t\t\taction = s.options.errorHandler(Key{}, numRequeues, err)\n   727→\t\tcase keyWorkItem:\n   728→\t\t\taction = s.options.errorHandler(entry.key, numRequeues, err)\n   729→\t\tdefault:\n   730→\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"keyQueue: unhandled entry %T\", entry))\n   731→\t\t}\n   732→\n   733→\t\tswitch action {\n   734→\t\tcase ErrorActionRetry:\n   735→\t\t\ts.wq.AddRateLimited(entry)\n   736→\t\tcase ErrorActionStop:\n   737→\t\t\ts.wq.ShutDown()\n   738→\t\tcase ErrorActionIgnore:\n   739→\t\t\ts.wq.Forget(entry)\n   740→\t\tdefault:\n   741→\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"keyQueue: unknown action %q from error handler %v\", action, s.options.errorHandler))\n   742→\t\t}\n   743→\t} else {\n   744→\t\t// As the object was processed successfully we can \"forget\" it.\n   745→\t\t// This clears any rate limiter state associated with this object, so\n   746→\t\t// it won't be throttled based on previous failure history.\n   747→\t\ts.wq.Forget(entry)\n   748→\t}\n   749→}\n   750→\n   751→// lastKnownObjects stores the last known state of an object from a subscriber's\n   752→// perspective. ccnpEvents == nil && ... {\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n}\n```\n\n**Key Patterns:**\n- Uses `resource.Resource[T]` to get event channels\n- `resource.Events(ctx)` returns `<-chan resource.Event[T]`\n- Event types: `resource.Sync`, `resource.Upsert`, `resource.Delete`\n- **Critical:** Must call `event.Done(err)` for each event - failure means no new events for that key\n- Sync events mark initial listing complete\n- Create intermediate representations (SlimCNP) when needed\n- Use atomic.Bool for synchronization flags\n\n---\n\n### 3. Resource.Resource[T] Pattern (pkg/k8s/resource/resource.go)\n\n**File:** `/workspace/pkg/k8s/resource/resource.go` (key excerpts)\n\n```go\n// Resource[T] interface - the core abstraction\ntype Resource[T k8sRuntime.Object] interface {\n\t// Observable interface (from stream.Observable)\n\tstream.Observable[Event[T]]\n\n\t// Events returns channel of events\n\t// Each event MUST be marked as handled with Done()\n\t// Missing Done() causes panic via finalizer\n\t//\n\t// Event sequence:\n\t// (start), Upsert*, Upsert*, (done replaying), Upsert, Upsert,\n\t//   (synced), Sync, Upsert, Delete, Upsert, ...\n\tEvents(ctx context.Context, opts ...EventsOpt) <-chan Event[T]\n\n\t// Store retrieves read-only store, blocks until synchronized\n\tStore(context.Context) (Store[T], error)\n}\n\n// Constructor function\nfunc New[T k8sRuntime.Object](\n\tlc cell.Lifecycle,\n\tlw cache.ListerWatcher,\n\topts ...ResourceOption,\n) Resource[T] {\n\tr := &resource[T]{lw: lw}\n\tr.opts.sourceObj = func() k8sRuntime.Object {\n\t\tvar obj T\n\t\treturn obj\n\t}\n\tfor _, o := range opts {\n\t\to(&r.opts)\n\t}\n\tr.ctx, r.cancel = context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n\tr.reset()\n\tlc.Append(r)\n\treturn r\n}\n\n// ResourceOption patterns - functional options\nfunc WithTransform[From, To k8sRuntime.Object](\n\ttransform func(From) (To, error),\n) ResourceOption {\n\treturn WithLazyTransform(\n\t\tfunc() k8sRuntime.Object {\n\t\t\tvar obj From\n\t\t\treturn obj\n\t\t},\n\t\tfunc(fromRaw any) (any, error) {\n\t\t\tif from, ok := fromRaw.(From); ok {\n\t\t\t\tto, err := transform(from)\n\t\t\t\treturn to, err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"expected %T, got %T\", nil, fromRaw)\n\t\t})\n}\n\nfunc WithMetric(scope string) ResourceOption {\n\treturn func(o *options) {\n\t\to.metricScope = scope\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc WithIndexers(indexers cache.Indexers) ResourceOption {\n\treturn func(o *options) {\n\t\to.indexers = indexers\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc WithName(name string) ResourceOption {\n\treturn func(o *options) {\n\t\to.name = name\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc WithStoppableInformer() ResourceOption {\n\treturn func(o *options) {\n\t\to.releasable = true\n\t}\n}\n\n// Event structure\ntype Event[T k8sRuntime.Object] struct {\n\tKind   EventKind  // Sync, Upsert, or Delete\n\tKey    Key        // resource.Key{Namespace, Name}\n\tObject T          // The actual object\n\tDone   func(error) // Must call when handled\n}\n\n// EventKind enum\nconst (\n\tSync EventKind   // Initial sync complete\n\tUpsert EventKind // Create or update\n\tDelete EventKind // Deletion\n)\n\n// Event options for tuning retry behavior\nfunc WithRateLimiter(r workqueue.RateLimiter) EventsOpt {\n\treturn func(o *eventsOpts) {\n\t\to.rateLimiter = r\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc WithErrorHandler(h ErrorHandler) EventsOpt {\n\treturn func(o *eventsOpts) {\n\t\to.errorHandler = h\n\t}\n}\n\n// ErrorHandler signature\n// (key, retryCount, error) -> ErrorAction\ntype ErrorHandler func(Key, int, error) ErrorAction\n\n// Default behavior: AlwaysRetry\nconst (\n\tErrorActionRetry  ErrorAction\n\tErrorActionStop   ErrorAction\n\tErrorActionIgnore ErrorAction\n)\n```\n\n**Usage Example:**\n```go\n// In a hive cell/constructor\nvar exampleCell = hive.Module(\n\t\"example\",\n\tcell.Provide(\n\t\tfunc(lc cell.Lifecycle, c k8sClient.Clientset) resource.Resource[*slim_corev1.Pod] {\n\t\t\tlw := utils.ListerWatcherFromTyped[*slim_corev1.PodList](\n\t\t\t\tc.Slim().CoreV1().Pods(\"\"),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t\treturn resource.New(\n\t\t\t\tlc, lw,\n\t\t\t\tresource.WithMetric(\"pods\"),\n\t\t\t\tresource.WithName(\"pods\"),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t},\n\t),\n)\n\n// Consuming the resource\nfunc usePods(pods resource.Resource[*slim_corev1.Pod]) {\n\tgo func() {\n\t\tfor event := range pods.Events(ctx) {\n\t\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n\t\t\tcase resource.Sync:\n\t\t\t\t// Initial sync complete\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\t\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\terr := onPodUpsert(event.Object)\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\terr := onPodDelete(event.Object)\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n}\n\n// Or use the store directly (blocks until synced)\nstore, err := pods.Store(ctx)\nallPods := store.List()\n```\n\n**Key Patterns:**\n- Lazy initialization (informer only starts when Events() or Store() called)\n- **CRITICAL:** Must call `event.Done(error)` - missing it causes panic via finalizer\n- Sync event signals initial replay of existing objects complete\n- Functional options for configuration\n- Support for object transformation (e.g., SlimCNP from full CNP)\n- Rate limiting and error handling for retries\n- Metrics collection support\n\n---\n\n### 4. Hive Cell Pattern for Controllers (operator/pkg/ciliumenvoyconfig/)\n\n**File:** `/workspace/operator/pkg/ciliumenvoyconfig/cell.go`\n\n```go\n// Cell is the hive module definition\nvar Cell = cell.Module(\n\t\"ciliumenvoyconfig\",\n\t\"Manages the CiliumEnvoyConfig controllers\",\n\n\t// Configuration structure with flags\n\tcell.Config(l7LoadBalancerConfig{\n\t\tLoadBalancerL7:          \"\",\n\t\tLoadBalancerL7Ports:     []string{},\n\t\tLoadBalancerL7Algorithm: \"round_robin\",\n\t}),\n\t\n\t// Register the controller setup function\n\tcell.Invoke(registerL7LoadBalancingController),\n)\n\n// Configuration structure with pflag.FlagSet integration\ntype l7LoadBalancerConfig struct {\n\tLoadBalancerL7          string\n\tLoadBalancerL7Algorithm string\n\tLoadBalancerL7Ports     []string\n}\n\nfunc (r l7LoadBalancerConfig) Flags(flags *pflag.FlagSet) {\n\tflags.String(\"loadbalancer-l7\", r.LoadBalancerL7, \n\t\t\"Enable L7 loadbalancer capabilities for services via L7 proxy. Applicable values: envoy\")\n\tflags.String(\"loadbalancer-l7-algorithm\", r.LoadBalancerL7Algorithm, \n\t\t\"Default LB algorithm for services that do not specify related annotation\")\n\tflags.StringSlice(\"loadbalancer-l7-ports\", r.LoadBalancerL7Ports, \n\t\t\"List of service ports that will be automatically redirected to backend.\")\n}\n\n// Parameter injection using cell.In\ntype l7LoadbalancerParams struct {\n\tcell.In\n\n\tLogger             logrus.FieldLogger\n\tCtrlRuntimeManager ctrlRuntime.Manager\n\tConfig             l7LoadBalancerConfig\n}\n\n// Invoke function - runs during hive startup\nfunc registerL7LoadBalancingController(params l7LoadbalancerParams) error {\n\tif params.Config.LoadBalancerL7 != \"envoy\" {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tparams.Logger.Info(\"Register Envoy load balancer reconciler\")\n\n\treconciler := newCiliumEnvoyConfigReconciler(\n\t\tparams.CtrlRuntimeManager.GetClient(),\n\t\tparams.Logger,\n\t\tparams.Config.LoadBalancerL7Algorithm,\n\t\tparams.Config.LoadBalancerL7Ports,\n\t\t10,\n\t\toperatorOption.Config.ProxyIdleTimeoutSeconds,\n\t)\n\n\tif err := reconciler.SetupWithManager(params.CtrlRuntimeManager); err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to setup Envoy load balancer reconciler: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n```\n\n**File:** `/workspace/operator/pkg/ciliumenvoyconfig/ciliumenvoyconfig.go`\n\n```go\n// Reconciler struct - implements controller-runtime Reconciler interface\ntype ciliumEnvoyConfigReconciler struct {\n\tclient client.Client\n\tlogger logrus.FieldLogger\n\n\talgorithm          string\n\tports              []string\n\tmaxRetries         int\n\tidleTimeoutSeconds int\n}\n\nfunc newCiliumEnvoyConfigReconciler(\n\tc client.Client,\n\tlogger logrus.FieldLogger,\n\tdefaultAlgorithm string,\n\tports []string,\n\tmaxRetries int,\n\tidleTimeoutSeconds int,\n) *ciliumEnvoyConfigReconciler {\n\treturn &ciliumEnvoyConfigReconciler{\n\t\tclient: c,\n\t\tlogger: logger,\n\t\talgorithm: defaultAlgorithm,\n\t\tports: ports,\n\t\tmaxRetries: maxRetries,\n\t\tidleTimeoutSeconds: idleTimeoutSeconds,\n\t}\n}\n\n// SetupWithManager - called from hive to register with controller-runtime\nfunc (r *ciliumEnvoyConfigReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager) error {\n\treturn ctrl.NewControllerManagedBy(mgr).\n\t\tFor(&corev1.Service{}).        // Watch Service resources\n\t\tOwns(&ciliumv2.CiliumEnvoyConfig{}). // Own CiliumEnvoyConfig resources\n\t\tComplete(r)                     // Install this as the reconciler\n}\n\n// Reconcile - the core reconciliation loop (implements controller-runtime Reconciler)\nfunc (r *ciliumEnvoyConfigReconciler) Reconcile(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\treq ctrl.Request,\n) (ctrl.Result, error) {\n\t// Create scoped logger with context\n\tscopedLog := r.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Controller: \"ciliumenvoyconfig\",\n\t\tlogfields.Resource:   req.NamespacedName,\n\t})\n\tscopedLog.Info(\"Starting reconciliation\")\n\n\tsvc := &corev1.Service{}\n\tif err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, svc); err != nil {\n\t\tif k8serrors.IsNotFound(err) {\n\t\t\tscopedLog.WithError(err).Debug(\"Unable to get service - either deleted or not yet available\")\n\t\t\treturn ctrl.Result{}, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn ctrl.Result{}, err\n\t}\n\n\tif isLBProtocolAnnotationEnabled(svc) || hasAnyPort(svc, r.ports) {\n\t\tif err := r.createOrUpdateEnvoyConfig(ctx, svc); Generates typed client code\n- `+k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces` - Generates DeepCopy implementations\n- `+deepequal-gen:private-method` - Generates custom equality checks (ignores LastAppliedConfig annotation)\n- `scope=\"Namespaced\"` - Resource is namespace-scoped\n- `+kubebuilder:subresource:status` - Separate status subresource\n- `+deepequal-gen=false` on TypeMeta/ObjectMeta - Skips generation for metadata fields\n- Methods include: `Parse()`, `GetIdentityLabels()`, `RequiresDerivative()`\n\n#### Example 2: CiliumClusterwideNetworkPolicy (Cluster-scoped)\n**File:** `/workspace/pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/ccnp_types.go`\n\n```go\n// +genclient\n// +genclient:nonNamespaced\n// +k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces=k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object\n// +deepequal-gen:private-method=true\n// +kubebuilder:resource:categories={cilium,ciliumpolicy},singular=\"ciliumclusterwidenetworkpolicy\",path=\"ciliumclusterwidenetworkpolicies\",scope=\"Cluster\",shortName={ccnp}\n// +kubebuilder:subresource:status\n// +kubebuilder:storageversion\ntype CiliumClusterwideNetworkPolicy struct {\n\t// +deepequal-gen=false\n\tmetav1.TypeMeta `json:\",inline\"`\n\t// +deepequal-gen=false\n\tmetav1.ObjectMeta `json:\"metadata\"`\n\n\tSpec *api.Rule `json:\"spec,omitempty\"`\n\tSpecs api.Rules `json:\"specs,omitempty\"`\n\tStatus CiliumNetworkPolicyStatus `json:\"status\"`\n}\n\n// Similar methods but with empty namespace handling for cluster-scoped resources\nfunc (r *CiliumClusterwideNetworkPolicy) Parse() (api.Rules, error) { ... }\n```\n\n**Key Differences:**\n- `+genclient:nonNamespaced` - Makes it cluster-scoped\n- `scope=\"Cluster\"` in kubebuilder resource tag\n- Empty namespace in Parse() method (cluster-wide resources have no namespace)\n\n#### Example 3: CiliumEnvoyConfig (Simpler CRD)\n**File:** `/workspace/pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/cec_types.go`\n\n```go\n// +genclient\n// +k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces=k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object\n// +kubebuilder:resource:categories={cilium},singular=\"ciliumenvoyconfig\",path=\"ciliumenvoyconfigs\",scope=\"Namespaced\",shortName={cec}\n// +kubebuilder:printcolumn:JSONPath=\".metadata.creationTimestamp\",description=\"The age of the identity\",name=\"Age\",type=date\n// +kubebuilder:storageversion\ntype CiliumEnvoyConfig struct {\n\t// +k8s:openapi-gen=false\n\t// +deepequal-gen=false\n\tmetav1.TypeMeta `json:\",inline\"`\n\t// +k8s:openapi-gen=false\n\t// +deepequal-gen=false\n\tmetav1.ObjectMeta `json:\"metadata\"`\n\n\tSpec CiliumEnvoyConfigSpec `json:\"spec,omitempty\"`\n}\n\ntype CiliumEnvoyConfigSpec struct {\n\tServices []*ServiceListener `json:\"services,omitempty\"`\n\tBackendServices []*Service `json:\"backendServices,omitempty\"`\n\tResources []XDSResource `json:\"resources,omitempty\"`\n\tNodeSelector *slim_metav1.LabelSelector `json:\"nodeSelector,omitempty\"`\n}\n\ntype Service struct {\n\tName string `json:\"name\"`\n\tNamespace string `json:\"namespace\"`\n\tPorts []string `json:\"number,omitempty\"`\n}\n```\n\n**Key Patterns:**\n- Simpler structure with only Spec (no Status)\n- `+k8s:openapi-gen=false` - Skip from OpenAPI schema\n- Nested types for better organization\n- Uses protobuf-compatible types (XDSResource with `*anypb.Any`)\n\n---\n\n### 2. map[k8s.ServiceID]map[resource.Key]struct{}\n}\n\n// Main event loop pattern\nfunc (p *policyWatcher) watchResources(ctx context.Context) {\n\tgo func() {\n\t\tvar knpEvents <-chan p.svcCacheNotifications\n\n\t\tfor {\n\t\t\tselect {\n\t\t\t// Each resource type has its own case\n\t\t\tcase event, ok := <-knpEvents:\n\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tknpEvents = {\n\t\t\t\t\tp.knpSynced.Store(true)\n\t\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t// Handle Upsert (create/update) and Delete\n\t\t\t\tvar err error\n\t\t\t\tswitch event.Kind <-cnpEvents:\n\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tcnpEvents = nil\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t// Create SlimCNP intermediate representation\n\t\t\t\tslimCNP :=   event.Object.Spec,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tSpecs:      event.Object.Specs,\n\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tresourceID := resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\t\terr = p.onDelete(slimCNP, event.Key, k8sAPIGroupCiliumNetworkPolicyV2, resourceID)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\treportCNPChangeMetrics(err)\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t// Exit when all channels closed\n\t\t\tif knpEvents == nil && cnpEvents == nil && ccnpEvents == nil && ... {\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n}\n```\n\n**Key Patterns:**\n- Uses `resource.Resource[T]` to get event channels\n- `resource.Events(ctx)` returns `<-chan resource.Event[T]`\n- Event types: `resource.Sync`, `resource.Upsert`, `resource.Delete`\n- **Critical:** Must call `event.Done(err)` for each event - failure means no new events for that key\n- Sync events mark initial listing complete\n- Create intermediate representations (SlimCNP) when needed\n- Use atomic.Bool for synchronization flags\n\n---\n\n### 3. Resource.Resource[T] Pattern (pkg/k8s/resource/resource.go)\n\n**File:** `/workspace/pkg/k8s/resource/resource.go` (key excerpts)\n\n```go\n// Resource[T] interface - the core abstraction\ntype Resource[T k8sRuntime.Object] interface {\n\t// Observable interface (from stream.Observable)\n\tstream.Observable[Event[T]]\n\n\t// Events returns channel of events\n\t// Each event MUST be marked as handled with Done()\n\t// Missing Done() causes panic via finalizer\n\t//\n\t// Event sequence:\n\t// (start), Upsert*, Upsert*, (done replaying), Upsert, Upsert,\n\t//   (synced), Sync, Upsert, Delete, Upsert, ...\n\tEvents(ctx context.Context, opts ...EventsOpt) <-chan Event[T]\n\n\t// Store retrieves read-only store, blocks until synchronized\n\tStore(context.Context) (Store[T], error)\n}\n\n// Constructor function\nfunc New[T k8sRuntime.Object](\n\tlc cell.Lifecycle,\n\tlw cache.ListerWatcher,\n\topts ...ResourceOption,\n) Resource[T] {\n\tr := &resource[T]{lw: lw}\n\tr.opts.sourceObj = func() k8sRuntime.Object {\n\t\tvar obj T\n\t\treturn obj\n\t}\n\tfor _, o := range opts {\n\t\to(&r.opts)\n\t}\n\tr.ctx, r.cancel = context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n\tr.reset()\n\tlc.Append(r)\n\treturn r\n}\n\n// ResourceOption patterns - functional options\nfunc WithTransform[From, To k8sRuntime.Object](\n\ttransform func(From) (To, error),\n) ResourceOption {\n\treturn WithLazyTransform(\n\t\tfunc() k8sRuntime.Object {\n\t\t\tvar obj From\n\t\t\treturn obj\n\t\t},\n\t\tfunc(fromRaw any) (any, error) {\n\t\t\tif from, ok := fromRaw.(From); ok {\n\t\t\t\tto, err := transform(from)\n\t\t\t\treturn to, err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"expected %T, got %T\", nil, fromRaw)\n\t\t})\n}\n\nfunc WithMetric(scope string) ResourceOption {\n\treturn func(o *options) {\n\t\to.metricScope = scope\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc WithIndexers(indexers cache.Indexers) ResourceOption {\n\treturn func(o *options) {\n\t\to.indexers = indexers\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc WithName(name string) ResourceOption {\n\treturn func(o *options) {\n\t\to.name = name\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc WithStoppableInformer() ResourceOption {\n\treturn func(o *options) {\n\t\to.releasable = true\n\t}\n}\n\n// Event structure\ntype Event[T k8sRuntime.Object] struct {\n\tKind   EventKind  // Sync, Upsert, or Delete\n\tKey    Key        // resource.Key{Namespace, Name}\n\tObject T          // The actual object\n\tDone   func(error) // Must call when handled\n}\n\n// EventKind enum\nconst (\n\tSync EventKind   // Initial sync complete\n\tUpsert EventKind // Create or update\n\tDelete EventKind // Deletion\n)\n\n// Event options for tuning retry behavior\nfunc WithRateLimiter(r workqueue.RateLimiter) EventsOpt {\n\treturn func(o *eventsOpts) {\n\t\to.rateLimiter = r\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc WithErrorHandler(h ErrorHandler) EventsOpt {\n\treturn func(o *eventsOpts) {\n\t\to.errorHandler = h\n\t}\n}\n\n// ErrorHandler signature\n// (key, retryCount, error) -> ErrorAction\ntype ErrorHandler func(Key, int, error) ErrorAction\n\n// Default behavior: AlwaysRetry\nconst (\n\tErrorActionRetry  ErrorAction\n\tErrorActionStop   ErrorAction\n\tErrorActionIgnore ErrorAction\n)\n```\n\n**Usage Example:**\n```go\n// In a hive cell/constructor\nvar exampleCell = hive.Module(\n\t\"example\",\n\tcell.Provide(\n\t\tfunc(lc cell.Lifecycle, c k8sClient.Clientset) resource.Resource[*slim_corev1.Pod] {\n\t\t\tlw := utils.ListerWatcherFromTyped[*slim_corev1.PodList](\n\t\t\t\tc.Slim().CoreV1().Pods(\"\"),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t\treturn resource.New(\n\t\t\t\tlc, lw,\n\t\t\t\tresource.WithMetric(\"pods\"),\n\t\t\t\tresource.WithName(\"pods\"),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t},\n\t),\n)\n\n// Consuming the resource\nfunc usePods(pods resource.Resource[*slim_corev1.Pod]) {\n\tgo func() {\n\t\tfor event := range pods.Events(ctx) {\n\t\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n\t\t\tcase resource.Sync:\n\t\t\t\t// Initial sync complete\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\t\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\terr := onPodUpsert(event.Object)\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\terr := onPodDelete(event.Object)\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n}\n\n// Or use the store directly (blocks until synced)\nstore, err := pods.Store(ctx)\nallPods := store.List()\n```\n\n**Key Patterns:**\n- Lazy initialization (informer only starts when Events() or Store() called)\n- **CRITICAL:** Must call `event.Done(error)` - missing it causes panic via finalizer\n- Sync event signals initial replay of existing objects complete\n- Functional options for configuration\n- Support for object transformation (e.g., SlimCNP from full CNP)\n- Rate limiting and error handling for retries\n- Metrics collection support\n\n---\n\n### 4. Hive Cell Pattern for Controllers (operator/pkg/ciliumenvoyconfig/)\n\n**File:** `/workspace/operator/pkg/ciliumenvoyconfig/cell.go`\n\n```go\n// Cell is the hive module definition\nvar Cell = cell.Module(\n\t\"ciliumenvoyconfig\",\n\t\"Manages the CiliumEnvoyConfig controllers\",\n\n\t// Configuration structure with flags\n\tcell.Config(l7LoadBalancerConfig{\n\t\tLoadBalancerL7:          \"\",\n\t\tLoadBalancerL7Ports:     []string{},\n\t\tLoadBalancerL7Algorithm: \"round_robin\",\n\t}),\n\t\n\t// Register the controller setup function\n\tcell.Invoke(registerL7LoadBalancingController),\n)\n\n// Configuration structure with pflag.FlagSet integration\ntype l7LoadBalancerConfig struct {\n\tLoadBalancerL7          string\n\tLoadBalancerL7Algorithm string\n\tLoadBalancerL7Ports     []string\n}\n\nfunc (r l7LoadBalancerConfig) Flags(flags *pflag.FlagSet) {\n\tflags.String(\"loadbalancer-l7\", r.LoadBalancerL7, \n\t\t\"Enable L7 loadbalancer capabilities for services via L7 proxy. Applicable values: envoy\")\n\tflags.String(\"loadbalancer-l7-algorithm\", r.LoadBalancerL7Algorithm, \n\t\t\"Default LB algorithm for services that do not specify related annotation\")\n\tflags.StringSlice(\"loadbalancer-l7-ports\", r.LoadBalancerL7Ports, \n\t\t\"List of service ports that will be automatically redirected to backend.\")\n}\n\n// Parameter injection using cell.In\ntype l7LoadbalancerParams struct {\n\tcell.In\n\n\tLogger             logrus.FieldLogger\n\tCtrlRuntimeManager ctrlRuntime.Manager\n\tConfig             l7LoadBalancerConfig\n}\n\n// Invoke function - runs during hive startup\nfunc registerL7LoadBalancingController(params l7LoadbalancerParams) error {\n\tif params.Config.LoadBalancerL7 != \"envoy\" {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tparams.Logger.Info(\"Register Envoy load balancer reconciler\")\n\n\treconciler := newCiliumEnvoyConfigReconciler(\n\t\tparams.CtrlRuntimeManager.GetClient(),\n\t\tparams.Logger,\n\t\tparams.Config.LoadBalancerL7Algorithm,\n\t\tparams.Config.LoadBalancerL7Ports,\n\t\t10,\n\t\toperatorOption.Config.ProxyIdleTimeoutSeconds,\n\t)\n\n\tif err := reconciler.SetupWithManager(params.CtrlRuntimeManager); err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to setup Envoy load balancer reconciler: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n```\n\n**File:** `/workspace/operator/pkg/ciliumenvoyconfig/ciliumenvoyconfig.go`\n\n```go\n// Reconciler struct - implements controller-runtime Reconciler interface\ntype ciliumEnvoyConfigReconciler struct {\n\tclient client.Client\n\tlogger logrus.FieldLogger\n\n\talgorithm          string\n\tports              []string\n\tmaxRetries         int\n\tidleTimeoutSeconds int\n}\n\nfunc newCiliumEnvoyConfigReconciler(\n\tc client.Client,\n\tlogger logrus.FieldLogger,\n\tdefaultAlgorithm string,\n\tports []string,\n\tmaxRetries int,\n\tidleTimeoutSeconds int,\n) *ciliumEnvoyConfigReconciler {\n\treturn &ciliumEnvoyConfigReconciler{\n\t\tclient: c,\n\t\tlogger: logger,\n\t\talgorithm: defaultAlgorithm,\n\t\tports: ports,\n\t\tmaxRetries: maxRetries,\n\t\tidleTimeoutSeconds: idleTimeoutSeconds,\n\t}\n}\n\n// SetupWithManager - called from hive to register with controller-runtime\nfunc (r *ciliumEnvoyConfigReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager) error {\n\treturn ctrl.NewControllerManagedBy(mgr).\n\t\tFor(&corev1.Service{}).        // Watch Service resources\n\t\tOwns(&ciliumv2.CiliumEnvoyConfig{}). // Own CiliumEnvoyConfig resources\n\t\tComplete(r)                     // Install this as the reconciler\n}\n\n// Reconcile - the core reconciliation loop (implements controller-runtime Reconciler)\nfunc (r *ciliumEnvoyConfigReconciler) Reconcile(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\treq ctrl.Request,\n) (ctrl.Result, error) {\n\t// Create scoped logger with context\n\tscopedLog := r.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Controller: \"ciliumenvoyconfig\",\n\t\tlogfields.Resource:   req.NamespacedName,\n\t})\n\tscopedLog.Info(\"Starting reconciliation\")\n\n\tsvc := &corev1.Service{}\n\tif err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, svc); err != nil {\n\t\tif k8serrors.IsNotFound(err) {\n\t\t\tscopedLog.WithError(err).Debug(\"Unable to get service - either deleted or not yet available\")\n\t\t\treturn ctrl.Result{}, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn ctrl.Result{}, err\n\t}\n\n\tif isLBProtocolAnnotationEnabled(svc) || hasAnyPort(svc, r.ports) {\n\t\tif err := r.createOrUpdateEnvoyConfig(ctx, svc); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn ctrl.Result{}, err\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tif err := r.deleteEnvoyConfig(ctx, svc); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn ctrl.Result{}, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog.Info(\"Successfully reconciled\")\n\treturn ctrl.Result{}, nil\n}\n```\n\n**Key Patterns:**\n- `cell.Module()` declares a hive module with name and description\n- `cell.Config()` registers configuration struct with automatic flag binding\n- Configuration type must implement `Flags(*pflag.FlagSet)` method\n- `cell.Invoke()` registers setup functions that run during hive startup\n- Parameter injection via `cell.In` struct tag for dependency injection\n- Reconciler implements `Reconcile(context.Context, ctrl.Request)` method\n- `SetupWithManager()` configures the controller:\n  - `For(&resource)` - watches primary resource\n  - `Owns(&resource)` - watches owned resources\n  - `Complete(reconciler)` - registers the reconciler\n- Controller-runtime auto-enqueues updates when watched resources change\n\n---\n\n### 5. c.cnpResource.Events(ctx)\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\tscopedLog.Info(\"Stopping PolicyQuotaController\")\n\t\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n\n\t\tcase event, ok := <-eventChan:\n\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\t// Channel closed\n\t\t\t\tscopedLog.Info(\"PolicyQuotaController event channel closed\")\n\t\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Handle the event based on its kind\n\t\t\tvar err error\n\t\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n\t\t\tcase resource.Sync:\n\t\t\t\t// Initial sync complete\n\t\t\t\tscopedLog.Debug(\"Initial policy list sync complete\")\n\n\t\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\terr = c.onPolicyUpsert(event.Object)\n\n\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\terr = c.onPolicyDelete(event.Object)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Mark the event as processed\n\t\t\t// If err is not nil, the event will be retried\n\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// onPolicyUpsert handles policy creation/update events.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) onPolicyUpsert(policy *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) error {\n\tnamespace := policy.GetNamespace()\n\tname := policy.GetName()\n\n\tc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer c.mu.Unlock()\n\n\t// Check if this is a new policy\n\toldCount := c.policyCounts[namespace]\n\n\t// Only increment if the policy wasn't already counted\n\t// (we detect this by checking if it's a new entry for this namespace)\n\tif oldCount == 0 || !c.policyExists(namespace, name) {\n\t\tc.policyCounts[namespace]++\n\t}\n\n\tnewCount := c.policyCounts[namespace]\n\n\tscopedLog := c.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Controller: \"PolicyQuotaController\",\n\t\t\"namespace\":         namespace,\n\t\t\"policy\":            name,\n\t\t\"count\":             newCount,\n\t\t\"max\":               c.maxPerNamespace,\n\t})\n\n\tif newCount > c.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\tscopedLog.Warn(\"Policy quota exceeded for namespace\")\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"policy quota exceeded: namespace %s has %d policies, max is %d\",\n\t\t\tnamespace, newCount, c.maxPerNamespace)\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog.Debug(\"Policy counted in namespace\")\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// onPolicyDelete handles policy deletion events.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) onPolicyDelete(policy *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) error {\n\tnamespace := policy.GetNamespace()\n\tname := policy.GetName()\n\n\tc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer c.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tif count, exists := c.policyCounts[namespace]; exists && count > 0 {\n\t\tc.policyCounts[namespace]--\n\t\tif c.policyCounts[namespace] == 0 {\n\t\t\tdelete(c.policyCounts, namespace)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tc.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Controller: \"PolicyQuotaController\",\n\t\t\"namespace\":         namespace,\n\t\t\"policy\":            name,\n\t\t\"count\":             c.policyCounts[namespace],\n\t}).Debug(\"Policy removed from namespace count\")\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// CheckQuota returns an error if the namespace has exceeded its policy quota.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\tc.mu.RLock()\n\tcount := c.policyCounts[namespace]\n\tc.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif count >= c.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"policy quota exceeded: namespace %s has %d policies, max is %d\",\n\t\t\tnamespace, count, c.maxPerNamespace)\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// GetPolicyCounts returns a snapshot of policy counts per namespace.\n// This is primarily for testing purposes.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) GetPolicyCounts() map[string]int {\n\tc.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer c.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\t// Return a copy to prevent external modification\n\tcounts := make(map[string]int, len(c.policyCounts))\n\tfor ns, count := range c.policyCounts {\n\t\tcounts[ns] = count\n\t}\n\treturn counts\n}\n\n// policyExists checks if a policy with the given namespace/name is already counted.\n// This is a helper method that must only be called while holding mu.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) policyExists(namespace, name string) bool {\n\t// In a real implementation, this would check against an actual policy store.\n\t// For now, we track by incrementing on upsert and decrementing on delete.\n\t// Since we're called only during upsert, we assume the count is accurate.\n\treturn true\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

Fix any issues found.\n\n## Phase 1: Identify Changes\n\nRun `git diff` (or `git diff HEAD` if there are staged changes) to see what changed. If there are no git changes, review the most recently modified files that the user mentioned or that you edited earlier in this conversation.\n\n## Phase 2: Launch Three Review Agents in Parallel\n\nUse the Agent tool to launch all three agents concurrently in a single message. Pass each agent the full diff so it has the complete context.\n\n### Agent 1: Code Reuse Review\n\nFor each change:\n\n1. **Search for existing utilities and helpers** that could replace newly written code. Use Grep to find similar patterns elsewhere in the codebase — common locations are utility directories, shared modules, and files adjacent to the changed ones.\n2. **Flag any new function that duplicates existing functionality.** Suggest the existing function to use instead.\n3. **Flag any inline logic that could use an existing utility** — hand-rolled string manipulation, manual path handling, custom environment checks, ad-hoc type guards, and similar patterns are common candidates.\n\n### Agent 2: Code Quality Review\n\nReview the same changes for hacky patterns:\n\n1. **Redundant state**: state that duplicates existing state, cached values that could be derived, observers/effects that could be direct calls\n2. **Parameter sprawl**: adding new parameters to a function instead of generalizing or restructuring existing ones\n3. **Copy-paste with slight variation**: near-duplicate code blocks that should be unified with a shared abstraction\n4. **Leaky abstractions**: exposing internal details that should be encapsulated, or breaking existing abstraction boundaries\n5. **Stringly-typed code**: using raw strings where constants, enums (string unions), or branded types already exist in the codebase\n\n### Agent 3: Efficiency Review\n\nReview the same changes for efficiency:\n\n1. **Unnecessary work**: redundant computations, repeated file reads, duplicate network/API calls, N+1 patterns\n2. **Missed concurrency**: independent operations run sequentially when they could run in parallel\n3. **Hot-path bloat**: new blocking work added to startup or per-request/per-render hot paths\n4. **Unnecessary existence checks**: pre-checking file/resource existence before operating (TOCTOU anti-pattern) — operate directly and handle the error\n5. **Memory**: unbounded data structures, missing cleanup, event listener leaks\n6. **Overly broad operations**: reading entire files when only a portion is needed, loading all items when filtering for one\n\n## Phase 3: Fix Issues\n\nWait for all three agents to complete. Aggregate their findings and fix each issue directly. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01C6bsHWW4b3nAEQQJjxXLGL","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"I see the issue now. The `policyExists` method is not really checking if a policy exists - it's just returning true. This is problematic because:\n\n1. During the initial Sync phase, we might get multiple Upsert events for policies being replayed\n2. The current logic tries to detect if a policy is new, but the `policyExists` check doesn't actually do anything meaningful\n\nLooking at the logic:\n```go\n// Only increment if the policy wasn't already counted\n// (we detect this by checking if it's a new entry for this namespace)\nif oldCount == 0 || !c.policyExists(namespace, name) {\n\tc.policyCounts[namespace]++\n}\n```\n\nThe condition `oldCount == 0 || !c.policyExists(namespace, name)` doesn't make sense because:\n1. If oldCount == 0, we increment (OK for first policy)\n2. But if oldCount > 0, we still check policyExists which always returns true\n3. So we never increment after the first policy\n\nThe real issue is that we need to maintain a cache of which policies we've seen. The simplest fix is to use a set of policy keys (namespace/name combinations) to track which policies we've already counted.\n\nLet me refactor the controller to properly track policies using a cache.","signature":"ErYKCkYICxgCKkBLiYz9UWaah5uWUHemHI2RuMZOEFj003lZ+MsYGSW21aszv0Ys/QXMkqFF78xHYLWPeDUJBiLZruLst0dNQNUDEgx8Y0YKjoMzCqMhR7kaDPDld4f1QM5ypmTxGyIwpPaUHlVIVMFyNNLsNBBGL0EwYO+XjKNq8hQS6ajZ184aQEXuSpnqsA2TdnoDJiakKp0JTrpggew5DUBzHcXajYlifBZi5frllDZV98OsU+JSwriBLK6xamNtLBGPnD5yVKF5OBbjiXHGuqpeH3Rg3Y63nJPYuPwH5rUom63SqvR0Hok83+TwTJS0YcDg88s5V33PQXFYUq3Qu9utQlr6gr3AqAXlTmYyskbz0YZC0bs82/FLnKwcSqtaA/uDCrKWiooL3dj6xuPmQJIq7SyT3jetM0Za2mo0+3Kef4M9OPY1pA3Kj+x9UlgDbP6BlijCoyux7fZgngaZIqzc62bqp3FDlPdeYfe46lbTm1kILxs1QI2oXBGZtJHOH3mi9Y90hHoDvWXt+WEEd/D7PIiCJKVHPPsLQ/IuBscKb3T+RZlKBu9+FCm6Qx786AiKaUrB9xlIxm1/tucMLUjse/FQq9muENXV2Zg7YleFI/XYFhuley+DjMW5Bt5rf6eEot8kvoa2nN74aJ1Kx4dGlgCnN80AyvTIfZDDgyZHcudVslC310FF9oGGAqyzrT33Ne/gLcwZqxyYZMSlsJHraT3kbtSskvQF4sZvxGWdACjI7hElC11doJNATH0SElT6+Iq2Ohkv6HMjvWC3JUmjD4VFpmpIAoIoulOfikjsuieNmweFAN1yLG9/ScyInK6br5q1kwzDDfF5uloVKpIRpwR9eVt5ivX02N9UhlrATqXrKzk0gf1yxCoXv/srRNhzrohEuhCl5GfOsXbprC1gM20Bi2P1cM1W82+voLdfaoNaJ6U7MNyFABgjsiJjeCERXbnha0ZO9gm9YHk4Ya3IGdNHfQjsPQetMvaTdTTLeeceRrn0nr/aYPcZPjK9rkce2Md1pTbPIkdLg2IzbkpZ9wDqA83tlqS2+LtosZWJ24MCrmYRMXPOR2Z7RVHmaFOxftY13+bMedMr5M1auS56LIwO+mdrWQOYeucncn1tbCuAloFYtU15Cn0JksJwILPVvvoGjO5XJZG8y02Enxta5ML/sGZ/nDrCQmt+dXOwcW0BKHXYHwPgN6rEzCxYYjRPR9du87Jlz0GoKsPwxcerO4RfyG3kK9rql2FpBtqS698bezt2luL8iYTdOq29aKgM3HCoTp4+2mp037WjdKbw8qi/4XqqgsFxE9sCIZj9C3pWMag6E1Fx8xF+jx8kuLpZv7Rp26WHIyAwRQMJiy1WC01T++cuhITj1k66r7aJ356F8mmJ2nQ9rtY9mcRWjG3x0I4QlhTk0BP7F0XsnNGGzjvcNuRfGasihvhYsFuHBFYcTwkimO1PqIP0gW1llPlop85B+fw6XbYWaPLsEyznBYsYhX2nxPnwu9LmcIT04hNx1JZjtoCUoNZdw6SPsh4wbEAT3J8q0i7QAAliuu7vT6TH/52YGZQAcqCh0/pQ0jr9062Hxu5V2uMuk+eA8/AF/uACvJsFiB7usw5fbszeN6b2G0tkSpIf/z5yH9MZPKu/JDVmTFnL2SHwi70mzaAKQVo7C2HkfnqCrsk5mwrT+mlhY081/0k8EB7dDAkGlSoIftxtaswcKIkbWfQivbBblzRXC2t6pTaJWbyvA7MCn4Q9UhryRsoKtV5HzeIfZXXC2/AYAQ=="}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3228,"cache_read_input_tokens":47196,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephe
